SAMPLE     Pure helium gas with purity 99.9% was used as the      C2131  1   12 
           target. The pressure of the helium gas in the chamber  C2131  1   13 
           was adjusted for the beam to stop completely inside    C2131  1   14 
           the chamber before reaching the detectors              C2131  1   15 
DETECTOR   (SI) Array of silicon detectors was placed inside the  C2131  1   16 
           chamber at angles ranging from 0deg to 60deg in steps  C2131  1   17 
           of 5deg to detect the recoiling alpha particles.       C2131  1   18 
METHOD     (TTM) The thick target inverse kinematics (TTIK)       C2131  1   19 
           technique was used                                     C2131  1   20 
ANALYSIS   Alpha particle energy was calculated from particle     C2131  1   21 
           kinematics. The spectra of alpha particles measured in C2131  1   22 
           the laboratory frame were converted into c.m.          C2131  1   23 
           excitation functions. Because of the extended gas      C2131  1   24 
           target, the scattering angle is not fixed and has to   C2131  1   25 
           be calculated from the energy of the recoil alpha      C2131  1   26 
           particle and the known location of the detectors.      C2131  1   27 
           The energy loss of an alpha particle and the solid     C2131  1   28 
           angle also depend on the location of the interaction   C2131  1   29 
           point and have to be calculated for each energy bin in C2131  1   30 
           the measured spectrum. This was done using a code whichC2131  1   31 
           takes into account the relevant experimental conditionsC2131  1   32 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S) Statistical uncertainty                        C2131  1   33
